 is khabar ne golmes parishad kii disha hi badal di

 log tivi ke zariye popular hone vaale baabaaon ke prabhaav main aa rahe hai

 iske alaava vahaan do sabase bade mudde the

 OBC and SC get fee waiver and scholarship

 ) August 14 holds a special place in the history of cricket
 yah din do diggajon se judaa hua he
 On this day, one expired and the other got ‘uplift’
 sanyog yah bhi he ki ye donon vaakye england main hue
 On this day in 1948, Don Bradman was bowled at zero in his last Test innings at the Oval
 duusari taraf aaj hi ke din manchester main sachin tendulkar ne apana pehla test shatak jamaaya
 August 14, 1948: Bradman needed just four runs to take his career average to 100 in the last Test innings
 england ke viruddh us test main australian diggaj duusari hi gend khelte hue bold ho gaye
 His dream wicket went to English legbreak googly bowler Eric Hollies
 breadman test kariyar main 7000 ran banane se bhi chook gaye
 Finally 99 in 52 Tests
 94 kii ausat se 6996 ran ke saath unhone cricket ko alavida kaha

 ’ gauratlab he ki kai channelon par prasaarit agsit pole main bijepi kii aguwai vaale endie ko bahumat milane kii bhavishyavaanee kii gai he

 unhone ek bayaan main prakritik sansadhano kii nilaamee rajasav bhagidaari yaa roylty ke aadhaar par karne kaa prastaav kiya he
 He said the auction would be a highly sustainable and transparent method based on revenue sharing or higher royalties of natural resources
 isse bhartiya udhyamiyon ko protsaahan milegaa, jo vishwastareey takanic laaenge, aadhunik kaarkaane kholenge or desh main bada nivesh laaenge

 iske baavjood use inke aayaat par arabon dollar kharch karne pad rahe hai
